# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes Controller Runtime Reconciler Registration

## Your Task

Trace how a controller registers itself with the controller-runtime Manager in kubernetes/kubernetes. Find the Go source files that define the Reconciler interface, implement SetupWithManager, and wire the controller into the manager's reconcile loop.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

67-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've created a comprehensive answer document at `/workspace/answer.json` that traces how controllers register themselves with the controller-runtime Manager in Kubernetes. Here's a summary of the key findings:

## Key Discoveries

### Controller Registration Pattern
Rather than using `SetupWithManager`, Kubernetes uses a **descriptor-based registration system**:

1. **ControllerDescriptor** - Encapsulates controller metadata and initialization logic
2. **InitFunc** - The function type that initializes and starts a controller
3. **ControllerContext** - Provides all necessary dependencies (clients, informers, config)
4. **controller.Interface** - The base interface all controllers implement

### The Registration Chain
```
Run() → StartControllers() → StartController() → InitFunc() → controller.Run()
```

### Critical Files
- **cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go** - Main orchestration
- **cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/core.go** - Controller implementations  
- **staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go** - Base interfaces

### Reconciler Pattern
Controllers also implement internal **Reconciler interfaces** for state reconciliation:
- Volume manager reconciler
- Plugin manager reconciler
- Attach/detach reconciler

The answer document includes all relevant files, symbols, the call chain, and a detailed narrative explanation of how the system works.

clientBuilder. rootClientBuilder is only used for\\n597: // the shared-informers client and token controller.\\n598: func CreateControllerContext(ctx context.Context, s *config.CompletedConfig, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder) (ControllerContext, error) {\\n599: \\t// Informer transform to trim ManagedFields for memory efficiency.\\n600: \\ttrim := func(obj interface{}) (interface{}, error) {\\n601: \\t\\tif accessor, err := meta.Accessor(obj); err == nil {\\n602: \\t\\t\\tif accessor.GetManagedFields() != nil {\\n603: \\t\\t\\t\\taccessor.SetManagedFields(nil)\\n604: \\t\\t\\t}\\n605: \\t\\t}\\n606: \\t\\treturn obj, nil\\n607: \\t}\\n608: \\n609: \\tversionedClient := time and fail only then. \\t\\tComponentConfig:                 s.ComponentConfig,\\n634: \\t\\tRESTMapper:                      restMapper,\\n635: \\t\\tInformersStarted:                make(chan struct{}),\\n636: controllerhealthz.NewMutableHealthzHandler(checks...)\n208: \n209: \t// Start the controller manager HTTP server\n210: \t// unsecuredMux is the handler for these controller *after* authn/authz filters have been applied\n211: \tvar unsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux\n212: \tif c.SecureServing != nil {\n213: \t\tunsecuredMux = genericcontrollermanager.NewBaseHandler(&c.ComponentConfig.Generic.Debugging, healthzHandler)\n214: \t\tslis.SLIMetricsWithReset{}.Install(unsecuredMux)\n215: \n216: \t\thandler := genericcontrollermanager.BuildHandlerChain(unsecuredMux, &c.Authorization, &c.Authentication)\n217: \t\t// TODO: handle stoppedCh and listenerStoppedCh returned by c.SecureServing.Serve\n218: \t\tif _, _, err := c.SecureServing.Serve(handler, 0, stopCh); err != nil {\n219: \t\t\treturn err\n220: \t\t}\n221: \t}\n222: \n223: \tclientBuilder, rootClientBuilder := createClientBuilders(c)\n224: \n225: \tsaTokenControllerDescriptor := newServiceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor(rootClientBuilder)\n226: \n227: \trun := func(ctx context.Context, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor) {\n228: \t\tcontrollerContext, err := CreateControllerContext(ctx, c, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder)\n229: \t\tif err != nil {\n230: \t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error building controller context\")\n231: \t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n232: \t\t}\n233: \n234: \t\tif err := StartControllers(ctx, controllerContext, controllerDescriptors, unsecuredMux, healthzHandler); err != nil {\n235: \t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error starting controllers\")\n236: \t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n237: \t\t}\n238: \n239: \t\tcontrollerContext.InformerFactory.Start(stopCh)\n240: \t\tcontrollerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory.Start(stopCh)\n241: \t\tclose(controllerContext.InformersStarted)\n242: \n243: \t\t<-ctx.Done()\n244: \t}\n245: \n246: \t// No leader election, run directly\n247: \tif !c.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.LeaderElect {\n248: \t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n249: \t\tcontrollerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController] = saTokenControllerDescriptor\n250: \t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n251: \t\treturn nil\n252: \t}\n253: \n254: \tid, err := os.Hostname()\n255: \tif err != nil {\n256: \t\treturn err\n257: \t}\n258: \n259: \t// add a uniquifier so that two processes on the same host don't accidentally both become active\n260: \tid = id + \"_\" + string(uuid.NewUUID())\n261: \n262: \t// leaderMigrator will be non-nil if and only if Leader Migration is enabled.\n263: \tvar leaderMigrator *leadermigration.LeaderMigrator = nil\n264: \n265: \t// If leader migration is enabled, create the LeaderMigrator and prepare for migration\n266: \tif leadermigration.Enabled(&c.ComponentConfig.Generic) {\n267: \t\tlogger.Info(\"starting leader migration\")\n268: \n269: \t\tleaderMigrator = leadermigration.NewLeaderMigrator(&c.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration,\n270: \t\t\t\"kube-controller-manager\")\n271: \n272: \t\t// startSATokenControllerInit is the original InitFunc.\n273: \t\tstartSATokenControllerInit := saTokenControllerDescriptor.GetInitFunc()\n274: \n275: \t\t// Wrap saTokenControllerDescriptor to signal readiness for migration after starting\n276: \t\t//  the controller.\n277: \t\tsaTokenControllerDescriptor.initFunc = func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller.Interface, bool, error) {\n278: \t\t\tdefer close(leaderMigrator.MigrationReady)\n279: \t\t\treturn startSATokenControllerInit(ctx, controllerContext, controllerName)\n280: \t\t}\n281: \t}\n282: \n283: \tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(kubefeatures.CoordinatedLeaderElection) {\n284: \t\tbinaryVersion, err := semver.ParseTolerant(featuregate.DefaultComponentGlobalsRegistry.EffectiveVersionFor(featuregate.DefaultKubeComponent).BinaryVersion().String())\n285: \t\tif err != nil {\n286: \t\t\treturn err\n287: \t\t}\n288: \t\temulationVersion, err := semver.ParseTolerant(featuregate.DefaultComponentGlobalsRegistry.EffectiveVersionFor(featuregate.DefaultKubeComponent).EmulationVersion().String())\n289: \t\tif err != nil {\n290: \t\t\treturn err\n291: \t\t}\n292: \n293: \t\t// Start lease candidate controller for coordinated leader election\n294: \t\tleaseCandidate, waitForSync, err := leaderelection.NewCandidate(\n295: \t\t\tc.Client,\n296: \t\t\t\"kube-system\",\n297: \t\t\tid,\n298: \t\t\t\"kube-controller-manager\",\n299: \t\t\tbinaryVersion.FinalizeVersion(),\n300: \t\t\temulationVersion.FinalizeVersion(),\n301: \t\t\tcoordinationv1.OldestEmulationVersion,\n302: \t\t)\n303: \t\tif err != nil {\n304: \t\t\treturn err\n305: \t\t}\n306: \t\thealthzHandler.AddHealthChecker(healthz.NewInformerSyncHealthz(waitForSync))\n307: \n308: \t\tgo leaseCandidate.Run(ctx)\n309: \t}\n310: \n311: \t// Start the main lock\n312: \tgo leaderElectAndRun(ctx, c, id, electionChecker,\n313: \t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.ResourceLock,\n314: \t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.ResourceName,\n315: \t\tleaderelection.LeaderCallbacks{\n316: \t\t\tOnStartedLeading: func(ctx context.Context) {\n317: \t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n318: \t\t\t\tif leaderMigrator != nil {\n319: \t\t\t\t\t// If leader migration is enabled, we should start only non-migrated controllers\n320: \t\t\t\t\t//  for the main lock.\n321: \t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors = filteredControllerDescriptors(controllerDescriptors, leaderMigrator.FilterFunc, leadermigration.ControllerNonMigrated)\n322: \t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"leader migration: starting main controllers.\")\n323: \t\t\t\t}\n324: \t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController] = saTokenControllerDescriptor\n325: \t\t\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n326: \t\t\t},\n327: \t\t\tOnStoppedLeading: func() {\n328: \t\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"leaderelection lost\")\n329: \t\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n330: \t\t\t},\n331: \t\t})\n332: \n333: \t// If Leader Migration is enabled, proceed to attempt the migration lock.\n334: \tif leaderMigrator != nil {\n335: \t\t// Wait for Service Account Token Controller to start before acquiring the migration lock.\n336: \t\t// At this point, the main lock must have already been acquired, or the KCM process already exited.\n337: \t\t// We wait for the main lock before acquiring the migration lock to prevent the situation\n338: \t\t//  where KCM instance A holds the main lock while KCM instance B holds the migration lock.\n339: \t\t<-leaderMigrator.MigrationReady\n340: \n341: \t\t// Start the migration lock.\n342: \t\tgo leaderElectAndRun(ctx, c, id, electionChecker,\n343: \t\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration.ResourceLock,\n344: \t\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration.LeaderName,\n345: \t\t\tleaderelection.LeaderCallbacks{\n346: \t\t\t\tOnStartedLeading: func(ctx context.Context) {\n347: \t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"leader migration: starting migrated controllers.\")\n348: \t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n349: \t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors = filteredControllerDescriptors(controllerDescriptors, leaderMigrator.FilterFunc, leadermigration.ControllerMigrated)\n350: \t\t\t\t\t// DO NOT start saTokenController under migration lock\n351: \t\t\t\t\tdelete(controllerDescriptors, names.ServiceAccountTokenController)\n352: \t\t\t\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n353: \t\t\t\t},\n354: \t\t\t\tOnStoppedLeading: func() {\n355: \t\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"migration leaderelection lost\")\n356: \t\t\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n357: \t\t\t\t},\n358: \t\t\t})\n359: \t}\n360: \n361: \t<-stopCh\n362: \treturn nil\n363: }\n364: \n365: // ControllerContext defines the context object for controller\n366: type ControllerContext struct {\n367: \t// ClientBuilder will provide a client for this controller to use\n368: \tClientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder\n369: \n370: \t// InformerFactory gives access to informers for the controller.\n371: \tInformerFactory informers.SharedInformerFactory\n372: \n373: \t// ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory gives access to informers for typed resources\n374: \t// and dynamic resources by their metadata. All generic controllers currently use\n375: \t// object metadata - if a future controller needs access to the full object this\n376: \t// would become GenericInformerFactory and take a dynamic client.\n377: \tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory informerfactory.InformerFactory\n378: \n379: \t// ComponentConfig provides access to init options for a given controller\n380: \tComponentConfig kubectrlmgrconfig.KubeControllerManagerConfiguration\n381: \n382: \t// DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper is a RESTMapper that will defer\n383: \t// initialization of the RESTMapper until the first mapping is\n384: \t// requested.\n385: \tRESTMapper *restmapper.DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper\n386: \n387: \t// InformersStarted is closed after all of the controllers have been initialized and are running.  After this point it is safe,\n388: \t// for an individual controller to start the shared informers. Before it is closed, they should not.\n389: \tInformersStarted chan struct{}\n390: \n391: \t// ResyncPeriod generates a duration each time it is invoked; this is so that\n392: \t// multiple controllers don't get into lock-step and all hammer the apiserver\n393: \t// with list requests simultaneously.\n394: \tResyncPeriod func() time.Duration\n395: \n396: \t// ControllerManagerMetrics provides a proxy to set controller manager specific metrics.\n397: \tControllerManagerMetrics *controllersmetrics.ControllerManagerMetrics\n398: \n399: \t// GraphBuilder gives an access to dependencyGraphBuilder which keeps tracks of resources in the cluster\n400: \tGraphBuilder *garbagecollector.GraphBuilder\n401: }\n402: \n403: // IsControllerEnabled checks if the context's controllers enabled or not\n404: func (c ControllerContext) IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor) bool {\n405: \tcontrollersDisabledByDefault := sets.NewString()\n406: \tif controllerDescriptor.IsDisabledByDefault() {\n407: \t\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault.Insert(controllerDescriptor.Name())\n408: \t}\n409: \treturn genericcontrollermanager.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor.Name(), controllersDisabledByDefault, c.ComponentConfig.Generic.Controllers)\n410: }\n411: \n412: // InitFunc is used to launch a particular controller. It returns a controller\n413: // that can optionally implement other interfaces so that the controller manager\n414: // can support the requested features.\n415: // The returned controller may be nil, which will be considered an anonymous controller\n416: // that requests no additional features from the controller manager.\n417: // Any error returned will cause the controller process to `Fatal`\n418: // The bool indicates whether the controller was enabled.\n419: type InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\n420: \n421: type ControllerDescriptor struct {\n422: \tname                      string\n423: \tinitFunc                  InitFunc\n424: \trequiredFeatureGates      []featuregate.Feature\n425: \taliases                   []string\n426: \tisDisabledByDefault       bool\n427: \tisCloudProviderController bool\n428: \trequiresSpecialHandling   bool\n429: }\n430: \n431: func (r *ControllerDescriptor) Name() string {\n432: \treturn r.name\n433: }\n434: \n435: func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetInitFunc() InitFunc {\n436: \treturn r.initFunc\n437: }\n438: \n439: func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetRequiredFeatureGates() []featuregate.Feature {\n440: \treturn append([]featuregate.Feature(nil), r.requiredFeatureGates...)\n441: }\n442: \n443: // GetAliases returns aliases to ensure backwards compatibility and should never be removed!\n444: // Only addition of new aliases is allowed, and only when a canonical name is changed (please see CHANGE POLICY of controller names)\n445: func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetAliases() []string {\n446: \treturn append([]string(nil), r.aliases...)\n447: }\n448: \n449: func (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsDisabledByDefault() bool {\n450: \treturn r.isDisabledByDefault\n451: }\n452: \n453: func (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsCloudProviderController() bool {\n454: \treturn r.isCloudProviderController\n455: }\n456: \n457: // RequiresSpecialHandling should return true only in a special non-generic controllers like ServiceAccountTokenController\n458: func map of named controller groups (you can start more than one in an init func)\n493: // paired to their ControllerDescriptor wrapper object that includes InitFunc.\n494: // This allows for structured downstream composition and subdivision.\n495: func NewControllerDescriptors() map[string]*ControllerDescriptor {\n496: \tcontrollers := map[string]*ControllerDescriptor{}\n497: \taliases := sets.NewString()\n498: \n499: \t// All the controllers must fulfil common constraints, or else we will explode.\n500: \tregister := func(controllerDesc *ControllerDescriptor) {\n501: \t\tif controllerDesc == nil {\n502: \t\t\tpanic(\"received nil controller for a registration\")\n503: \t\t}\n504: \t\tname := controllerDesc.Name()\n505: \t\tif len(name) == 0 {\n506: \t\t\tpanic(\"received controller without a name for a registration\")\n507: \t\t}\n508: \t\tif _, found := controllers[name]; found {\n509: \t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller name %q was registered twice\", name))\n510: \t\t}\n511: \t\tif controllerDesc.GetInitFunc() == nil {\n512: \t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q does not have an init function\", name))\n513: \t\t}\n514: \n515: \t\tfor _, alias := range controllerDesc.GetAliases() {\n516: \t\t\tif aliases.Has(alias) {\n517: \t\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q has a duplicate alias %q\", name, alias))\n518: \t\t\t}\n519: \t\t\taliases.Insert(alias)\n520: \t\t}\n521: \n522: \t\tcontrollers[name] = controllerDesc\n523: \t}\n524: \n525: \t// First add \"special\" controllers that aren't initialized normally. \tregister(newEndpointsControllerDescriptor())\n534: \tregister(newEndpointSliceControllerDescriptor())\n535: \tregister(newEndpointSliceMirroringControllerDescriptor())\n536: \tregister(newReplicationControllerDescriptor())\n537: \tregister(newPodGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n538: \tregister(newResourceQuotaControllerDescriptor())\n539: \tregister(newDaemonSetControllerDescriptor())\n543: \tregister(newJobControllerDescriptor())\n544: \tregister(newDeploymentControllerDescriptor())\n545: \tregister(newReplicaSetControllerDescriptor())\n546: \tregister(newHorizontalPodAutoscalerControllerDescriptor())\n547: \tregister(newDisruptionControllerDescriptor())\n548: \tregister(newStatefulSetControllerDescriptor())\n549: \tregister(newCronJobControllerDescriptor())\n550: \tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestSigningControllerDescriptor())\n551: \tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestApprovingControllerDescriptor())\n552: \tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n553: \tregister(newTTLControllerDescriptor())\n554: \tregister(newBootstrapSignerControllerDescriptor())\n555: \tregister(newTokenCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n556: \tregister(newNodeIpamControllerDescriptor())\n557: \tregister(newNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor())\n558: \n559: \tregister(newServiceLBControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n560: \tregister(newClusterRoleAggregrationControllerDescriptor())\n568: \tregister(newPersistentVolumeClaimProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n569: \tregister(newSELinuxWarningControllerDescriptor())\n585: \n586: \tfor _, alias := range aliases.UnsortedList() {\n587: \t\tif _, ok := controllers[alias]; ok {\n588: \t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"alias %q conflicts with a controller name\", alias))\n589: \t\t}\n590: \t}\n591: \n592: \treturn controllers\n593: }\n594: \n595: // CreateControllerContext creates a context struct containing references to resources needed by the\n596: // controllers such as the cloud provider and clientBuilder. rootClientBuilder is only used for\n597: // the shared-informers client and token controller.\n598: func CreateControllerContext(ctx context.Context, s *config.CompletedConfig, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder) (ControllerContext, error) {\n599: \t// Informer transform to trim ManagedFields for memory efficiency.\n600: \ttrim := func(obj interface{}) (interface{}, error) {\n601: \t\tif accessor, err := meta.Accessor(obj); err == nil {\n602: \t\t\tif accessor.GetManagedFields() != nil {\n603: \t\t\t\taccessor.SetManagedFields(nil)\n604: \t\t\t}\n605: \t\t}\n606: \t\treturn obj, nil\n607: \t}\n608: \n609: \tversionedClient := rootClientBuilder.ClientOrDie(\"shared-informers\")\n610: \tsharedInformers := informers.NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions(versionedClient, ResyncPeriod(s)(), informers.WithTransform(trim))\n611: \n612: \tmetadataClient := metadata.NewForConfigOrDie(rootClientBuilder.ConfigOrDie(\"metadata-informers\"))\n613: \tmetadataInformers := metadatainformer.NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions(metadataClient, ResyncPeriod(s)(), metadatainformer.WithTransform(trim))\n614: \n615: \t// If apiserver is not running we should wait for some time and fail only then. This is particularly\n616: \t// important when we start apiserver and controller manager at the same time.\n617: \tif err := genericcontrollermanager.WaitForAPIServer(versionedClient, 10*time.Second); err != nil {\n618: \t\treturn ControllerContext{}, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to wait for apiserver being healthy: %v\", err)\n619: \t}\n620: \n621: \t// Use a discovery client capable of being refreshed.\n622: \tdiscoveryClient := rootClientBuilder.DiscoveryClientOrDie(\"controller-discovery\")\n623: \tcachedClient := cacheddiscovery.NewMemCacheClient(discoveryClient)\n624: \trestMapper := restmapper.NewDeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper(cachedClient)\n625: \tgo wait.Until(func() {\n626: \t\trestMapper.Reset()\n627: \t}, 30*time.Second, ctx.Done())\n628: \n629: \tcontrollerContext := ControllerContext{\n630: \t\tClientBuilder:                   clientBuilder,\n631: \t\tInformerFactory:                 sharedInformers,\n632: \t\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory: informerfactory.NewInformerFactory(sharedInformers, metadataInformers),\n633: \t\tComponentConfig:                 s.ComponentConfig,\n634: \t\tRESTMapper:                      restMapper,\n635: \t\tInformersStarted:                make(chan struct{}),\n636: \t\tResyncPeriod:                    ResyncPeriod(s),\n637: \t\tControllerManagerMetrics:        controllersmetrics.NewControllerManagerMetrics(\"kube-controller-manager\"),\n638: \t}\n639: \n640: \tif controllerContext.ComponentConfig.GarbageCollectorController.EnableGarbageCollector &&\n641: \t\tcontrollerContext.IsControllerEnabled(NewControllerDescriptors()[names.GarbageCollectorController]) {\n642: \t\tignoredResources := make(map[schema.GroupResource]struct{})\n643: \t\tfor _, r := range controllerContext.ComponentConfig.GarbageCollectorController.GCIgnoredResources {\n644: \t\t\tignoredResources[schema.GroupResource{Group: r.Group, Resource: r.Resource}] = struct{}{}\n645: \t\t}\n646: \n647: \t\tcontrollerContext.GraphBuilder = garbagecollector.NewDependencyGraphBuilder(\n648: \t\t\tctx,\n649: \t\t\tmetadataClient,\n650: \t\t\tcontrollerContext.RESTMapper,\n651: \t\t\tignoredResources,\n652: \t\t\tcontrollerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory,\n653: \t\t\tcontrollerContext.InformersStarted,\n654: \t\t)\n655: \t}\n656: \n657: \tcontrollersmetrics.Register()\n658: \treturn controllerContext, nil\n659: }\n660: \n661: // StartControllers starts a set of controllers with a specified ControllerContext\n662: func StartControllers(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor,\n663: \tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux, healthzHandler *controllerhealthz.MutableHealthzHandler) error {\n664: \tvar controllerChecks []healthz.HealthChecker\n665: \n666: \t// Always start the SA token controller first using a full-power client, since it needs to mint tokens for the rest\n667: \t// If this fails, just return here and fail since other controllers won't be able to get credentials.\n668: \tif serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, ok := controllerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController]; ok {\n669: \t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, unsecuredMux)\n670: \t\tif err != nil {\n671: \t\t\treturn err\n672: \t\t}\n673: \t\tif check != nil {\n674: \t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n675: \t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n676: \t\t}\n677: \t}\n678: \n679: \t// Each controller is passed a context where the logger has the name of\n680: \t// the controller set through WithName. That name then becomes the prefix of\n681: \t// of all log messages emitted by that controller.\n682: \t//\n683: \t// In StartController, an explicit \"controller\" key is used instead, for two reasons:\n684: \t// - while contextual logging is alpha, klog.LoggerWithName is still a no-op,\n685: \t//   so we cannot rely on it yet to add the name\n686: \t// - it allows distinguishing between log entries emitted by the controller\n687: \t//   and those emitted for it - this is a bit debatable and could be revised.\n688: \tfor _, controllerDesc := range controllerDescriptors {\n689: \t\tif controllerDesc.RequiresSpecialHandling() {\n690: \t\t\tcontinue\n691: \t\t}\n692: \n693: \t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, controllerDesc, unsecuredMux)\n694: \t\tif err != nil {\n695: \t\t\treturn err\n696: \t\t}\n697: \t\tif check != nil {\n698: \t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n699: \t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, kubernetes/kubernetes, controllers register themselves with the controller manager through a descriptor-based initialization pattern rather than the `SetupWithManager` pattern used in controller-runtime.\\n\\n## Core Components\\n\\n### 1. **ControllerDescriptor** (controllermanager.go:421-429)\\nDescribes a controller with metadata including:\\n- `name`: Controller identifier\\n- `initFunc`: Function that initializes and starts the controller\\n- `aliases`: Backward-compatible names\\n- `requiredFeatureGates`: Feature gates needed\\n- `isDisabledByDefault`: Whether the controller is disabled by default\\n- `isCloudProviderController`: Whether this is a cloud provider-specific controller\\n\\n### 2. **InitFunc Type** (controllermanager.go:419)\\n```go\\ntype InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\\n```\\nThe InitFunc is the equivalent of `SetupWithManager` - it's responsible for:\\n- Creating the controller instance\\n- Configuring event handlers and informers\\n- Starting the controller's reconciliation loop\\n- Returning whether the controller was enabled and any errors\\n\\n### 3. **ControllerContext** (controllermanager.go:366-401)\\nProvides controllers with necessary resources:\\n- `ClientBuilder`: For creating API clients\\n- `InformerFactory`: For creating informers to watch Kubernetes resources\\n- `ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory`: For watching typed and dynamic resources\\n- `ComponentConfig`: Controller-specific configuration\\n- `RESTMapper`: For mapping resources to REST endpoints\\n- `InformersStarted`: Channel signaling when informers have started\\n- `ResyncPeriod`: Function generating periodic resync intervals\\n- `ControllerManagerMetrics`: For tracking controller metrics\\n- `GraphBuilder`: For garbage collector dependency tracking\\n\\n### 4. **controller.Interface** (staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go:25-55)\\nThe base interface that all controllers must implement:\\n- `Name() string`: Returns the controller's canonical name\\n- Optional `Debuggable` interface: Provides debugging HTTP handlers\\n- Optional `HealthCheckable` interface: Provides health check endpoints\\n\\n## Controller Registration Flow\\n\\n### Step 1: Descriptor Definition\\nEach controller is defined through a `newXxxControllerDescriptor()` function. For example, in core.go:\\n```go\\nfunc newEndpointsControllerDescriptor() *ControllerDescriptor {\\n    return &ControllerDescriptor{\\n        name:     names.EndpointsController,\\n        aliases:  []string{\\\"endpoint\\\"},\\n        initFunc: startEndpointsController,\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### Step 2: Controller Initialization\\nThe `initFunc` (e.g., `startEndpointsController`) is called to initialize the controller:\\n```go\\nfunc startEndpointsController(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller.Interface, bool, error) {\\n    go endpointcontroller.NewEndpointController(\\n        ctx,\\n        controllerContext.InformerFactory.Core().V1().Pods(),\\n        controllerContext.InformerFactory.Core().V1().Services(),\\n        controllerContext.InformerFactory.Core().V1().Endpoints(),\\n        controllerContext.ClientBuilder.ClientOrDie(\\\"endpoint-controller\\\"),\\n        controllerContext.ComponentConfig.EndpointController.EndpointUpdatesBatchPeriod.Duration,\\n    ).Run(ctx, int(controllerContext.ComponentConfig.EndpointController.ConcurrentEndpointSyncs))\\n    return nil, true, nil\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### Step 3: Manager Registration\\nControllers are registered in `NewControllerDescriptors()` (controllermanager.go:495-593):\\n```go\\nregister(newEndpointsControllerDescriptor())\\nregister(newEndpointSliceControllerDescriptor())\\n// ... more controller registrations\\n```\\n\\n### Step 4: Starting Controllers\\nThe `StartControllers()` function (controllermanager.go:662-706) iterates through registered controllers and calls `StartController()` for each.\\n\\n`StartController()` (controllermanager.go:708-767):\\n- Checks if controller is enabled\\n- Calls the controller's `InitFunc`\\n- Registers health checkers\\n- Mounts any debugging handlers\\n\\n## Reconciliation Pattern\\n\\nKubernetes controllers use the **Reconciler** pattern internally for state reconciliation. Examples include:\\n\\n### Volume Manager Reconciler (pkg/kubelet/volumemanager/reconciler/reconciler_common.go:49-51)\\n```go\\ntype Reconciler interface {\\n    Starts running the reconciliation loop which executes periodically, checks\\n    if volumes that should be mounted are mounted and volumes that should\\n    not be mounted are unmounted.\\n    Run(stopCh <-chan struct{})\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### Plugin Manager Reconciler (pkg/kubelet/pluginmanager/reconciler/reconciler.go:37-41)\\n```go\\ntype Reconciler interface {\\n    Run starts running the reconciliation loop which executes periodically,\\n    checks if plugins are correctly registered or unregistered.\\n    Run(stopCh <-chan struct{})\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### Attach/Detach Controller Reconciler (pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go:301-305)\\nThe attach/detach controller uses a reconciler to periodically reconcile the desired and actual state of volume attachments:\\n```go\\nreconciler reconciler.Reconciler\\n```\\n\\n## Key Differences from controller-runtime\\n\\nWhile the Kubernetes native controllers don't use the `SetupWithManager` pattern from controller-runtime, they achieve the same goals through:\\n\\n1. **ControllerDescriptor** instead of SetupWithManager: Encapsulates controller metadata and initialization logic\\n2. **InitFunc** instead of imperative setup: Declarative function that returns the initialized controller\\n3. **ControllerContext** instead of Manager: Provides all necessary dependencies and resources\\n4. **controller.Interface** instead of reconciler.Reconciler: Base interface for all controller types\\n5. **Explicit Manager Loop**: The `Run()` function in controllermanager.go orchestrates controller startup and lifecycle\\n\\nThis design allows Kubernetes to manage many heterogeneous controllers with different initialization patterns and dependencies while maintaining a consistent registration and lifecycle management system.\"\n}\n",
